through a layered approach combining middleware, decorators, and template tags. The validation chain is initiated by CsrfViewMiddleware, which is the central CSRF protection mechanism in django/middleware/csrf.py. When a request is processed, CsrfViewMiddleware.process_view() is called, which validates incoming POST requests by checking the CSRF token. The core validation logic resides in the _check_token() method, which retrieves the CSRF secret from either a session or cookie and compares it against the submitted token. The critical security component is the _does_token_match() function (line 143-157 in django/middleware/csrf.py) which prevents timing attacks by using constant_time_compare() from django/utils/crypto.py. This function delegates to secrets.compare_digest(), which performs constant-time comparison to ensure attackers cannot infer token values through timing analysis. Token generation and masking are handled by _mask_cipher_secret() and _unmask_cipher_token() functions, which implement a cipher-based masking scheme to protect the token when rendered in the DOM. The get_token() function generates or retrieves tokens, while rotate_token() updates tokens on authentication events for enhanced security. The csrf_protect decorator in django/views/decorators/csrf.py provides per-view CSRF protection by wrapping CsrfViewMiddleware functionality. The template layer is supported by the csrf_token template tag in django/template/defaulttags.py through the CsrfTokenNode class, which renders a hidden input field containing the CSRF token for inclusion in POST forms. The complete protection chain ensures tokens are validated in constant time to prevent timing attacks, securely generated, properly masked when displayed, and rotated when necessary for maximum security.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":11,"cache_creation_input_tokens":882,"cache_read_input_tokens":66546,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":882},"output_tokens":3,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"2b9ec96b-fea0-4eba-9339-581f9b029217","uuid":"4508e12e-db66-44fe-838e-3e39863436f4"}

through a layered approach combining middleware, decorators, and template tags. The validation chain is initiated by CsrfViewMiddleware, which is the central CSRF protection mechanism in django/middleware/csrf.py. When a request is processed, CsrfViewMiddleware.process_view() is called, which validates incoming POST requests by checking the CSRF token. The core validation logic resides in the _check_token() method, which retrieves the CSRF secret from either a session or cookie and compares it against the submitted token. The critical security component is the _does_token_match() function (line 143-157 in django/middleware/csrf.py) which prevents timing attacks by using constant_time_compare() from django/utils/crypto.py. This function delegates to secrets.compare_digest(), which performs constant-time comparison to ensure attackers cannot infer token values through timing analysis. Token generation and masking are handled by _mask_cipher_secret() and _unmask_cipher_token() functions, which implement a cipher-based masking scheme to protect the token when rendered in the DOM. The get_token() function generates or retrieves tokens, while rotate_token() updates tokens on authentication events for enhanced security. The csrf_protect decorator in django/views/decorators/csrf.py provides per-view CSRF protection by wrapping CsrfViewMiddleware functionality. The template layer is supported by the csrf_token template tag in django/template/defaulttags.py through the CsrfTokenNode class, which renders a hidden input field containing the CSRF token for inclusion in POST forms. The complete protection chain ensures tokens are validated in constant time to prevent timing attacks, securely generated, properly masked when displayed, and rotated when necessary for maximum security.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
